---
title: Rahn Monitor API | Adverse Media
---

import { Tab, Tabs } from "nextra-theme-docs";

# Adverse Media

This endpoint returns a JSON object that returns the 100 most recent adverse media reports based on a search term.


```
https://api.rahnmonitor.co.za/adversemedia
```

## Path Parameters

| Parameter |  Type  | Description                                                                                            | Required? | Default |
| :-------: | :----: | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :-------: | :-----: |
|  apikey   | string | API Key for RahnMonitor |    Yes    |         |
|  query | string | Search term to search for | Yes | |

## Request Samples

<Tabs items={["JavaScript", "Python","Curl"]}>
  <Tab>
    <>
        ```js
        import axios from "axios";
        
        const url = "https://api.rahnmonitor.co.za/adversemedia?apikey=MYAPIKEY&query=Jacob%20Zuma";
        const data = async () => {
            try {
                const { data } = await axios.get(url, 
                    {
                        headers: {
                            "Content-Type": "application/json",
                        },
                    }
                );
                return data;
            } catch (err) {
                throw new Error(err.message);
            }
        };

        console.log(data);
        ```
    </>

  </Tab>
  <Tab>
    <>
        ```python
        import requests
        
        url = "https://api.rahnmonitor.co.za/adversemedia?apikey=MYAPIKEY&query=Jacob%20Zuma"
        response = requests.get(url)
        data = response.json()

        print(data)
        ```
    </>
  </Tab>
  <Tab>
    <>
        ```bash
        curl -X 'GET' \
        'https://api.rahnmonitor.co.za/adversemedia?apikey=MYAPIKEY&query=Jacob%20Zuma' \
        -H 'accept: application/json'
        ```
    </>
  </Tab>
</Tabs>
